if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'cd616fe812a127cdb4f3b1d30352435f27c17834') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'cd616fe812a127cdb4f3b1d30352435f27c17834') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5363857df46ebfa3109787e821e2527a3b9e66f4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'cd616fe812a127cdb4f3b1d30352435f27c17834') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'a8aebbcd382fe77b91671283f64a58d9eb0ddd93') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'a8aebbcd382fe77b91671283f64a58d9eb0ddd93') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '7e15c6824e74072ee90d417e2141d6e655e1c9a7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'a8aebbcd382fe77b91671283f64a58d9eb0ddd93') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != 'b4c111dcfbc1b44e3a1a09f7367e603e028b73d7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'b4c111dcfbc1b44e3a1a09f7367e603e028b73d7') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '7385c54c9cb6ff4294b128c866ba8f56f4e81c4c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'b4c111dcfbc1b44e3a1a09f7367e603e028b73d7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'c1a4dad83df0915196aebb017d40d29f32fee1e5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c1a4dad83df0915196aebb017d40d29f32fee1e5') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '3db683ea19fc10db2e745585b86e48dfde197c53') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c1a4dad83df0915196aebb017d40d29f32fee1e5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('polyfill.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: polyfill.min.js.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('polyfill.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): polyfill.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') != '4b1db283f599893469a0b1ebc411080657c3df71') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): polyfill.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('polyfill.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of polyfill.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') !== '4b1db283f599893469a0b1ebc411080657c3df71') {
		if (@sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') !== 'cefd82f604a18998bec4c4018edf8c6eb999bd61') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: polyfill.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('polyfill.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('polyfill.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('polyfill.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') !== '4b1db283f599893469a0b1ebc411080657c3df71') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): polyfill.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1182\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1182') err('Could not write to .version.php!');
